             <div class="carousel-caption">
              <h3>
               National Tournaments
              </h3>
              <div class="caption-description">
               <div class="main-listing-detail">
                <b>
                 TravelBall National Championship
                </b>
                <div class="setHeight">
                 <p>
                  The TravelBall National Championship (TNC) has emerged to become the biggest and most competitive tournament for ages 9 - 14U teams in the country.
												The TNCS (Travelball National Championship Series) events are used to qualify teams to play in the TNC.  
												In addition to the TNC, Nations Baseball has numerous National Tournament opportunities for teams wishing 
												to play a prestigious and fun National Tournament.  Play on the Florida Gulf Coast, Texas Gulf Coast or the Hill Country area of New Braunsfels,
												 TX just to name a few.
                  <a href="http://championships.nations-baseball.com/" target="_blank">
                   Click here
                  </a>
                  to see the lineup for this year's National Tournaments.

            <div class="item">
             <a href="/aces">
              <img alt="" class="img-responsive" height="500" src="/layouts/images/banner/baseball/acesslider.png" width="750"/>
             </a>
             <div class="carousel-caption">
              <h3>
               ACES Nation
              </h3>
              <div class="caption-description">
               <div class="main-listing-detail">
                <p>
                 <b>
                  Attack Your Future Like The Ball!!!
                 </b>
                </p>
                <div class="setHeight">
                 <p>
                  It is never too early to start thinking about your student's future and what you are going to do about college.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  <i>
                   Your 5 key questions will boil down to the following:
                  </i>
                  <br/>
                  <strong>
                   <ol>
                    <li>
                     What college will my student want to attend?
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     Is my student-athlete going to be willing, wanting and able to play in college?
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     With college admissions becoming ultra-competitive, will my student even be able to get in?
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     If my student does not get accepted to where we want, what will we do?
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     The total cost of attendance has gotten so high, no matter where my student goes, how will we pay for it?
                    </li>
                   </ol>
                  </strong>
                  Nations Baseball knows that college can be a difficult, stressful and challenging issue for many families.  As such, to help you become more knowledgable and prepared for the college process, Nations Baseball has teamed up with ACES Nation.  ACES Nation is a complete system for families with young student-athletes ranging in age from 5 to 17.  Their focus is to provide you with the education and knowledge necessary to improve your student-athletes personal growth and development and to increase the chances for them to go to college.  In addition to providing eductaional tools and resorces in the areas of sports nutrition, sports performance, college recruiting and college planning, as an ACES Nation member benefit, you will also receive private college scholarships to currently 340 colleges and universities with a maximum potential of $3,000 annually.
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  If you are concerned about your child's future,
                  <a href="/general/aces">
                   Click Here
                  </a>
                 </p>

And not only better, but with General Liability coverage so comprehensive that players, coaches, umpires, league officers/directors, and even volunteers are covered. All players and coaches are covered for secondary accident medical, too! Coverage for other organizations events, team practices, most fundraisers and team meetings as well. With support from the best in the business, Chappell Insurance. The insurance package is so good and so inexpensive that we have teams registering for Nations Baseball in areas where we are still growing!!!

              <h3>
               Metro Leagues
              </h3>
              <div class="caption-description">
               <div class="main-listing-detail">
                <b>
                 Affordable
                </b>
                <div class="setHeight">
                 <p>
                  The strength of baseball is that every child can play. Nations Baseball understands that the recreational player is the 
											cornerstone of youth baseball. If kids are provided an affordable opportunity to play, they will build team teamwork and love of the game, 
											not just bat last and play every other inning. We have taken our bulk buying power to provide local leagues with an amazing package that can save 
											thousands of dollars in wasted fees that can go right back into your community. Will we dictate to you with rules and restrictions? No. 
											Your community knows best what your kids need. We provide a structure for you to run your league, the opportunity for tournament play, 
											and some amazing web tools to help run your league. And then we get off your back. Sound good?
